{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{____type_8h_ac6c55e737799b5e73899ccfae13b98e4}{vsf\+\_\+err\+\_\+t}} \+\_\+\+\_\+vsf\+\_\+eda\+\_\+call\+\_\+eda\+\_\+ex\+\_\+prepare (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{arm_2type_8h_a09674b9e56fd7a93a2169aa9210deec7}{uintptr\+\_\+t}}}]{func,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{arm_2type_8h_a09674b9e56fd7a93a2169aa9210deec7}{uintptr\+\_\+t}}}]{param,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{struct____vsf__eda__frame__state__t}{\+\_\+\+\_\+vsf\+\_\+eda\+\_\+frame\+\_\+state\+\_\+t}}}]{state,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{arm_2type_8h_af6a258d8f3ee5206d682d799316314b1}{bool}}}]{is\+\_\+sub\+\_\+call }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
please NEVER do following things. If param is NULL, please let frame-\/$>$param to be NULL
\end{DoxyNote}
if (NULL == param) \{ frame-\/$>$param = pthis; //!$<$ point to the current eda \} else \{ frame-\/$>$param = param; \}\mbox{\Hypertarget{vsf__eda_8h_aa7ca83ced2011bdd1871c064807f60e7}\label{vsf__eda_8h_aa7ca83ced2011bdd1871c064807f60e7}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{vsf__eda_8h_a6d43c223342139ca7521a3285e2c7dd2}\label{vsf__eda_8h_a6d43c223342139ca7521a3285e2c7dd2}}

\index{\_\_vsf\_eda\_call\_fsm@{\_\_vsf\_eda\_call\_fsm}!vsf\_eda.h@{vsf\_eda.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{\_\_vsf\_eda\_call\_fsm()}{\_\_vsf\_eda\_call\_fsm()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{vsf__fsm_8h_ae61ab5e1d66a489d89fa8786e6b5f64b}{fsm\+\_\+rt\+\_\+t}} \+\_\+\+\_\+vsf\+\_\+eda\+\_\+call\+\_\+fsm (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{vsf__eda_8h_a869fe5732129390c11e4c405bcb6c281}{vsf\+\_\+fsm\+\_\+entry\+\_\+t}}}]{entry,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{arm_2type_8h_a09674b9e56fd7a93a2169aa9210deec7}{uintptr\+\_\+t}}}]{param,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{linux_2include_2sys_2types_8h_a7c94ea6f8948649f8d181ae55911eeaf}{size\+\_\+t}}}]{local\+\_\+size }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item if VSF\+\_\+\+ERR\+\_\+\+NOT\+\_\+\+ENOUGH\+\_\+\+RESOURCES is detected, yield and try it again (automatically). For tasks sharing the same frame pool, if the pool is too small, only task performance will be affected, and all sub-\/task call will work when frame is allocated.
\item if the frame is allocated and pushed to the stack, we should yield to let the sub-\/task run.
\end{DoxyItemize}
\end{DoxyNote}
Since in either way, we will yield, no need to handle the return value of vsf\+\_\+eda\+\_\+call().\mbox{\Hypertarget{vsf__eda_8h_a78d37b47214056cf02dd04f250f5999d}\label{vsf__eda_8h_a78d37b47214056cf02dd04f250f5999d}}
